Harshpreet Singh JoharHarshpreet Singh Johar You You Upcoming Software Engineer Intern @Intuit | Executive board member @PEC ACM CSS | ReactJS, NEXT, MERN, FlutterUpcoming Software Engineer Intern @Intuit | Executive board member @PEC ACM CSS | ReactJS, NEXT, MERN, Flutter
2d 2d
Hey everyone,

Have you ever come across the meme "me vs the guy she told me not to worry about"? It's a humorous way to compare two people and showcase the difference in their abilities.

Well, I couldn't help but notice how this meme could also be applied to our GitHub contribution charts! The GitHub contribution chart is a great way to track your activity on the platform and identify areas for improvement.

So, in this context, "me" would be represented by a skilled and experienced developer's GitHub chart, and "the guy she told me not to worry about" would be represented by someone who may not be as experienced but is still employed in the industry.

And just like the meme, the comparison can be made between the two charts to see who has made more contributions. But the goal here isn't to belittle or mock someone. It's about using our GitHub contribution charts as a tool to motivate ourselves and push us to become better developers.

So, let's take a moment to reflect on our own GitHub charts and see if there's any room for improvement. And if you feel like your chart is lagging behind that of the "me" in the meme, don't worry! Everyone has to start somewhere. Just keep practicing and making contributions, and who knows, maybe one day you'll become the highly sought-after developer that everyone wants to work with.

Happy coding!
